(******************************************************************************************

 The conjunction of formulas of partial setoids

 In this file, we construct the conjunction in the category of partial setoids. Here we
 use the characterization of subobjects in terms of formulas as given in the file
 `SubobjectDispCat.v`.

 The construction of the connectives of subobjects of partial setoids is similar to how
 connectives are defined for subsets. For the conjunction, we reuse the conjunction of the
 first-order hyperdoctrine.

 Content
 1. The formula
 2. Elimination rules
 3. Introduction rule
 4. Stability under substitution
 5. Fiberwise binary products

 ******************************************************************************************)

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))]
⊢ (ψ₁ ∧ ψ₂) [π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))]
  ⇒ π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ)) ~ π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))

        
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))]
∧ (ψ₁ ∧ ψ₂) [π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))]
⊢ π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ)) ~ π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
(⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))])
[π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]
⊢ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))) ~
  π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))
  ⇒ (ψ₁ ∧ ψ₂) [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
    ⇒ (ψ₁ ∧ ψ₂) [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

    Defined.

    (** * 2. Elimination rules *)
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
per_subobject_mor_law (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
  per_subobject_conj ψ₁

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
per_subobject_mor_law (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
  per_subobject_conj ψ₁

      
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
(⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))])
[π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]
⊢ (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))),
   π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)) ⟩]
  ⇒ per_subobject_conj
    [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
    ⇒ ψ₁ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ
(⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))])
[π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]
∧ (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))),

  [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
  ⇒ ψ₁ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

    (** * 3. Introduction rule *)
    Context {χ : per_subobject Γ}
            (p : per_subobject_mor_law (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₁)
            (q : per_subobject_mor_law (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₂).

  per_subobject_conj

  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₂
(⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ))])

⊢ (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))),
   π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)) ⟩]
  ⇒ χ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
    ⇒ per_subobject_conj [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

q: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₂
(id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
[⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))),
 π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)) ⟩]
⊢ χ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
  ⇒ per_subobject_conj [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

      
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂, χ: per_subobject Γ
p: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₁
q: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₂
(id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ)
[⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))),
 π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)) ⟩]
∧ χ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
⊢ per_subobject_conj [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

      
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: partial_setoid H
ψ₁, ψ₂, χ: per_subobject Γ
p: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₁
q: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₂
(π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Γ)) ~ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Γ)))
[⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))),
 π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)) ⟩]
∧ χ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
⊢ (ψ₁ ∧ ψ₂) [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

ψ₁, ψ₂, χ: per_subobject Γ

  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₁
q: per_subobject_mor_law
  (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ) χ ψ₂
π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))) ~
π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))
∧ χ [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ)))]
⊢ ψ₁ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]
  ∧ ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ) ×h Γ))]

    Qed.
  End Conjunction.

  (** * 4. Stability under substitution *)
  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: partial_setoid H
s: partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁ Γ₂
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ₂
per_subobject_mor_law (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁)
  (per_subobject_conj (per_subobject_subst s ψ₁)
     (per_subobject_subst s ψ₂))
  (per_subobject_subst s (per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂))

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: partial_setoid H
s: partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁ Γ₂
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ₂
per_subobject_mor_law (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁)
  (per_subobject_conj (per_subobject_subst s ψ₁)
     (per_subobject_subst s ψ₂))
  (per_subobject_subst s (per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂))

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: partial_setoid H
s: partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁ Γ₂
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ₂
(⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h Γ₁))])
[π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))]
⊢ (id_partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁)
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))),
   π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)) ⟩]
  ⇒ (per_subobject_conj (per_subobject_subst s ψ₁)
       (per_subobject_subst s ψ₂))
    [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)))]
    ⇒ (per_subobject_subst s
         (per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂))
      [π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))]

       [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)),
        π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)) ⟩])
      [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
         [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,

           [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
         π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩]))
 [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂))]
 ∧ (∃h ((s
         [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)),
          π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)) ⟩])
        [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
           [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
         π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩]
        ∧ (ψ₂ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂))])
          [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
             [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂))

           π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩]))

      [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))),

     [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂))])
∧ (s
   [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)) ⟩])
  [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
     [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
   π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩]
  ∧ (ψ₁ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂))])
    [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
       [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩]

   π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)) ⟩ ]tm ~
  (π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₁)))
  [⟨ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))),
   π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)) ⟩ ]tm)
 [(π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)))
  [π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm]
 ∧ s
   [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
    [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
       [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
     [π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
     ]tm ]tm]
   ∧ ψ₁
     [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)))
      [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
         [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
       π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
       [π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
       ]tm ]tm])
∧ s
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
   [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
      [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
    π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
    [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)))
       [π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
       ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
    ]tm ]tm]
  ∧ ψ₂
    [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)))
     [⟨ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁))))
        [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
      π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
      [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)))
         [π₁
            (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
         ]tm,
       π₂ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
      ]tm ]tm]
⊢ ∃h (s
      [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)),
       π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
       [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)))
          [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
        π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
        [⟨ ((π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)))
            [π₁
               (tm_var
                  ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
            ]tm)
           [π₁
              (tm_var
                 (((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)
                  ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
         π₂
           (tm_var
              (((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
         ⟩ ]tm ]tm]
      ∧ ψ₁
        [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)))
         [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)))
            [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
          π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
          [⟨ ((π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)))
              [π₁
                 (tm_var
                    ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
              ]tm)
             [π₁
                (tm_var
                   (((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)
                    ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
           π₂
             (tm_var
                (((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)
                 ×h Γ₂)) ⟩ ]tm ]tm]
        ∧ ψ₂
          [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h Γ₂)))
           [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁)))
              [π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂))
              ]tm,
            π₂ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)) ⟩
            [⟨ ((π₁ (tm_var (((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂)))
                [π₁
                   (tm_var
                      ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))
                ]tm)
               [π₁
                  (tm_var
                     (((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)
                      ×h Γ₂)) ]tm,
             π₂
               (tm_var
                  (((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)
                   ×h Γ₂)) ⟩ ]tm ]tm])

        (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)))): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₁
γ₂:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₂
γ₂':= π₂ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₂
(γ₁ ~ γ₁' ∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂ ⟩] ∧ ψ₁ [γ₂])
∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂' ⟩] ∧ ψ₂ [γ₂'] ⊢ s [⟨ ?x, γ₂' ⟩]

γ₁ ~ γ₁' ∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂ ⟩] ∧ ψ₁ [γ₂] ⊢ s [⟨ γ₁', γ₂ ⟩]

(γ₁ ~ γ₁' ∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂ ⟩] ∧ ψ₁ [γ₂])
∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂' ⟩] ∧ ψ₂ [γ₂'] ⊢ ψ₂ [γ₂']
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: partial_setoid H
s: partial_setoid_morphism Γ₁ Γ₂
ψ₁, ψ₂: per_subobject Γ₂
γ₁:= π₂
  (π₁
     (π₁
        (π₁
           (tm_var
              ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))))): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₁
γ₁':= π₂
  (π₁
     (π₁
        (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)))): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₁
γ₂:= π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂))): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₂
γ₂':= π₂ (tm_var ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂)): tm ((((𝟙 ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₁) ×h Γ₂) ×h Γ₂) Γ₂
r: (γ₁ ~ γ₁' ∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂ ⟩] ∧ ψ₁ [γ₂])
∧ s [⟨ γ₁, γ₂' ⟩] ∧ ψ₂ [γ₂'] ⊢ γ₂ ~ γ₂'
ψ₂ [γ₂'] ⊢ ψ₂ [γ₂']

        apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.
  Qed.

  (** * 5. Fiberwise binary products *)
  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
fiberwise_binproducts
  (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
fiberwise_binproducts
  (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H)

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
locally_propositional (disp_cat_per_subobject H)
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H,
(disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
→ (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
  → (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(φ ψ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
?and Γ φ ψ -->[ identity Γ] φ
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(φ ψ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
?and Γ φ ψ -->[ identity Γ] ψ
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(φ ψ χ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
χ -->[ identity Γ] φ
→ χ -->[ identity Γ] ψ → χ -->[ identity Γ] ?and Γ φ ψ
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(s : category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧)
(φ ψ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ₂}]),
(disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ₁}]
⟦ ?and Γ₁
    (pr1 (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s φ))
    (pr1 (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s ψ)),
pr1
  (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s
     (?and Γ₂ φ ψ)) ⟧

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
locally_propositional (disp_cat_per_subobject H)
 apply locally_prop_disp_cat_per_subobject.
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H,
(disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
→ (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
  → (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: category_of_partial_setoids H
ψ₁, ψ₂: (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
(disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]

      exact (per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂).
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(φ ψ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
(λ (Γ0 : category_of_partial_setoids H)
 (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ0}]),
 per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ φ ψ -->[ identity Γ] φ
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: category_of_partial_setoids H
ψ₁, ψ₂: (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
(λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
 (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
 per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ ψ₁ ψ₂ -->[ identity Γ] ψ₁

      exact (per_subobject_conj_elim_left ψ₁ ψ₂).
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(φ ψ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
(λ (Γ0 : category_of_partial_setoids H)
 (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ0}]),
 per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ φ ψ -->[ identity Γ] ψ
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: category_of_partial_setoids H
ψ₁, ψ₂: (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
(λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
 (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
 per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ ψ₁ ψ₂ -->[ identity Γ] ψ₂

      exact (per_subobject_conj_elim_right ψ₁ ψ₂).
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(φ ψ χ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
χ -->[ identity Γ] φ
→ χ -->[ identity Γ] ψ
  → χ -->[
    identity Γ] (λ (Γ0 : category_of_partial_setoids H)
                 (ψ₁
                  ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ0}]),
                 per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ φ ψ
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: category_of_partial_setoids H
ψ₁, ψ₂, χ: (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]
p: χ -->[ identity Γ] ψ₁
q: χ -->[ identity Γ] ψ₂
χ -->[
identity Γ] (λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
             (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
             per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ ψ₁ ψ₂

      exact (per_subobject_conj_intro ψ₁ ψ₂ p q).
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
(s : category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧)
(φ ψ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ₂}]),
(disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ₁}]
⟦ (λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
   (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
   per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ₁
    (pr1 (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s φ))
    (pr1 (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s ψ)),
pr1
  (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s
     ((λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
       (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
       per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ₂ φ ψ)) ⟧
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: category_of_partial_setoids H
s: category_of_partial_setoids H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
ψ₁, ψ₂: (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ₂}]
(disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ₁}]
⟦ (λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
   (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
   per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ₁
    (pr1
       (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s ψ₁))
    (pr1
       (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s ψ₂)),
pr1
  (disp_cat_per_subobject_cleaving H Γ₂ Γ₁ s
     ((λ (Γ : category_of_partial_setoids H)
       (ψ₁ ψ₂ : (disp_cat_per_subobject H)[{Γ}]),
       per_subobject_conj ψ₁ ψ₂) Γ₂ ψ₁ ψ₂)) ⟧

      exact (per_subobject_conj_subst s ψ₁ ψ₂).
  Defined.
End Conjunction.
